CASIA 2.0 groundtruth dataset: https://github.com/namtpham/casia2groundtruth/
Backup link to the original dataset: https://goo.gl/4Q7bJW

IMPORTANT: Please notice that the authors made several mistakes in naming the files. 
I recommend you to use the commands in the excel file to rename the tampered files.

If you have any question, please don't hesistate to contact me at thanhnamvnu@gmail.com

If you use the groundtruth dataset for a scientific publication, please cite the following papers:

----------------
CASIA 2 dataset:
----------------

@inproceedings{dong2013casia,
  title={Casia image tampering detection evaluation database},
  author={Dong, Jing and Wang, Wei and Tan, Tieniu},
  booktitle={2013 IEEE China Summit and International Conference on Signal and Information Processing},
  pages={422--426},
  year={2013},
  organization={IEEE}
}

  title={Hybrid Image-Retrieval Method for Image-Splicing Validation},

  journal={Symmetry},
  volume={11},
  number={1},
  pages={83},

  publisher={Multidisciplinary Digital Publishing Institute}
}
